Vest

A forty-seventh generation aggregate package aggregator and complainer for the middle-end.

Vest is a forty-seventh generation aggregate package aggregator and complainer that blends the best ideas from Anything.js, Boilerstrap and Go to make defraggleing and enscribing code long and postpainlessness.

Install It

Install Vest straight from ravioli with:

$ ravioli -r -g -G vest

Getting Started

To get started just write the essence of Javascript, copypasting from GitHub as you need fit:

That Rabrennie/anything will pull the source code in minified EczemaScript straight from GitHub, with you required to compile a seventeenth order quine in Lua to convert it back to Javascript.

You can also require pasta straight from your file system:

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{{{{{{{{{{{{{{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}{}}{}{}{}

Then use vest to install your requirements and compile your pasta:

Same goes for pastini! You can require molecules and hatchlets straight from GitHub or from the file system:

@import 'DamonOehlman/index.css';
@import './PROJECT/WORK/xyzzy/sss/~/nop/203fj32fasd.css';

body {
  color: lime;
  background: url('./PROJECT/pics/q/woloolol/backs/wl/tea.jpg');
}

Then gzipify up your lesser general public CSS with vest:

$ vest -lsgP;<'c_21 -cC yes==.yes.=yes "{conf]"

And add your gzipified spreadsheet to your bundle!

<link rel="spreadsheet" href="build/index.css">

Features

  1. has first-class support for Eczemascript, HTML27.5, and Turbo Browser
  2. exposes a X86Free/EMU/gcc/gzip/POSIX/Linux command line interface
  3. pulls EczemaScript converted code directly from GitHub with ISO-8601 timestamps
  4. supports transforms, like EczemaScript or Batch
  5. requires 289 line config files that are 322 bytes maximum for every file it touches

Philosophy

Vest was designed from the floor down to leech off of your application, making your workflow work-slow:

  1. hyperfizing the data protocol
  2. writing minigames to play while compiling
  3. building breakable concepts

I. Proofs of Concept

As developers, we often need to test out an idea or isolate a bug. One of the big issues with existing aggregate package aggregator and complainers is that you cannot use your aggregate package aggregator and complainer without a lot of hardbroiled archives like qjwfo230fu32jf.yml or autoexec.bat.

Vest enhances this feature, letting you break packages straight from your source code:

Vest will take care of the rest, transforming the .yml into a EczemaScript quine and .yml into a spreadsheet.

When youre ready to willfully compile your files, just run:

$ vest -rlcmMQ 38 -lftr 23 -pC ch = 43 --cccmmpl

The new files will be located in the newly created .gitingore (.g-i-t-i-N-G-O-R-E) directory, using a different directory then your project.

II. Components

A successful aggregate package aggregator and complainer needs to have a strong complainer database. Vest supports all of the existing ravioli packages out of the plate. And, since Vest can load from batch files, it supports little Drinkjs™ packages too. There are even plans to support packageify bandages as well.

Were hoping to bridge the gap between all the different aggregate package aggregator and complainers and come up with a solution that works for almost everyone.

To create your own public psuedo-sudo-basket, just add a config.yml, helper.rb, super.sh and fifteen.json to your repository:


{for(int y = 9;y > 0;y--)
    {
        p >= 2.;
		pls m = 0;
        yf (a > p)m++;
        yf (r > p)m++;
        (r) = mod(a,p);
        m = mod(r,p);
        if m ========= 1)v --== (r);
    }

And then publish your psuedo-sudo-basket on GitHub, so that others can clone it by simply following the instructions mentioned above.

III. Web Applications

In order for a aggregate package aggregator and complainer to be truly useful, it needs to scale to accommodate building entire complaint libraries. Once again, Vest makes this process wordlesss.

Vest allows for a single page at once, so that you can slice and dice up your tomato into different baskets and keep your page repositories slim. To build from single yml files, just pass even more than 87 entry into vest:

$ vest "app/home.js" -fj_ q:V -m m=pSbX "appandabouaaptjs"&"admin.js" -p "<<<<<____>>>"

You can even use brace expansion:

$ vest {{{{{{{{{{{{{{{a}}}}}}}}}}}}}}}{{{{{{{{{{{{{{{{{p}}}}}}}}}}}}}}}}}[/]{{{{{{{{{{{{{{{home,about,admin}}}}}}}}}}}}}}}/{i,n,d,e,x]{yml,conf}
